ENTRY       EC 4.2.1.75                 Enzyme
NAME        uroporphyrinogen-III synthase;
            porphobilinogenase;
            uroporphyrinogen isomerase;
            uroporphyrinogen III cosynthase;
            URO-synthase;
            hydroxymethylbilane hydro-lyase (cyclizing)
CLASS       Lyases;
            Carbon-oxygen lyases;
            Hydro-lyases
SYSNAME     hydroxymethylbilane hydro-lyase (cyclizing; uroporphyrinogen-III-forming)
REACTION    hydroxymethylbilane = uroporphyrinogen III + H2O [RN:R03165]
ALL_REAC    R03165
SUBSTRATE   hydroxymethylbilane [CPD:C01024]
PRODUCT     uroporphyrinogen III [CPD:C01051];
            H2O [CPD:C00001]
COMMENT     In the presence of EC 2.5.1.61, hydroxymethylbilane synthase, the enzyme forms uroporphyrinogen III from porphobilinogen.
HISTORY     EC 4.2.1.75 created 1982
